Location: 38.58, -121.49282
Code: 2
Type: Outside mural
Address: 1108 R St, Sacramento, CA 95811
Name of location: Warehouse Artist Lofts
More location information: Hanging mist is made up of 72 perforated aluminum panels painted in soft layers of color, making up two walls of the inner courtyard of WAL, located at R and 11th Streets in Sacramento. The designs are inspired by the material itself, perforated aluminum panels with 50% open space; art that is half there, half absent. Dependent on the viewer’s angle to the work and the lighting on the panels, the paintings appear vibrant and opaque, or dissolve into their surroundings, barely visible.
Artist: Hennessy Christophel and Sofia Lacin
Name of project: Hanging Mist
Media coverage:
Instagram: https://www.instagram.com/p/ts0G1kjxt_/
